Important Foreign Telegrams 64

Germany's New Election Tactics 65

The National Socialist Party Uses Airplane Noise to Obstruct Speeches

The Socialist Party Also Sends Planes Into the Sky to Create the Appearance of Collisions

The Atmosphere in Various Locations Is Very Different Than Usual

Flags Flutter in a Multitude of Colors

Austria Simultaneously Holds Provincial Council Re-elections

National News Agency, Berlin, 23rd – Tonight in Berlin, over a hundred public gatherings will conclude the Prussian parliamentary election campaign. In total, during this twelve-day campaign period,

Page 6

there were 1,345 public gatherings held. The three open-air rallies separately convened by the National Socialist Party, the Communist Party, and the Socialist Party are not included in this number, which shows how intense the competition is. The Socialist Party's open-air rally held this morning was actually embellished by a bloodless battle in the sky and set a record for an unprecedented event in election history. After the rally began, the National Socialist Party's propaganda plane came to circle at low altitude, using the rumbling

of the engine to obstruct the speakers' voices. Unexpectedly, after the plane had only flown two laps, a Socialist Party propaganda plane returned. Seeing this, it urgently steered the plane forward, repeatedly feigning collisions. The National Socialist Party's plane, indeed not tolerating the intimidation, eventually left. The main speaker at this rally was the Prussian Premier Braun, a strong opponent of the National Socialist Party, hence this unprecedented bizarre scene. Tonight, Braun will also speak on the radio broadcast, making a final stand. As for this election campaign, in Berlin and various provinces, up to tonight, there have been no major disturbances. The number of people arrested by the police for engaging in minor conflicts is also not very high. The most significant incident was that a group of National Socialist Party members in Cologne attacked a Socialist Party leader and a police chief, leading to a brawl. The disturbance only subsided after the police arrived and made arrests. Both leaders went to the hospital for treatment.

National News Agency, Berlin, 23rd – Today is the day before the re-elections for the Prussian, Bavarian, and Württemberg state parliaments. The election campaigns of various parties have reached their peak. According to news from various locations, no major incidents have yet occurred, with only minor conflicts in Munich and a few other places, resulting in 30 injuries. According to recent indications, after this Prussian parliamentary re-election, it is feared that none of the parties will be able to win a majority of seats. Perhaps it will be like the federal parliament, with a dictatorial system established and the entire house controlled by a joint committee. National Socialist Party leader Hitler has asked for the support of women, promising that the party will improve family life in the future, making married life happier than it is today, and making the status of mothers more respected. However, the opposition parties ridiculed this by pointing out that the party has not even one female candidate for parliament, so how can it talk about expanding women's rights? In addition, religious issues have also been used as material for election speeches.

National News Agency, Berlin, 24th – Today, five-sixths of Germany is voting to re-elect the parliaments of Prussia, Bavaria, and Württemberg. Although German voters have voted three times in the past six weeks, the enthusiasm has not diminished at all.

National News Agency, Berlin, 24th – Today, German President Hindenburg also personally went to the election office near the presidential palace to vote, accompanied by his son. However, his son, being a soldier, had no right to vote and did not vote. When the German president entered and exited the election office, countless people gathered in the nearby streets, cheering and congratulating him, as this was the first time he had appeared among the people since being elected. Premier Brüning voted nearby in the village of Ashaburg in southern Germany and immediately drove back to Geneva. Ashaburg has the ancient castle of the Solms-Braunfels dynasty, and although it is surrounded by Bavarian territory, the village is still part of the Prussian state, hence Brüning went there to vote.

Reuters, Berlin, 24th – Because the parties have nominated so many candidates this time, the final results of the parliamentary elections will not be announced until 3 AM tomorrow morning. In this election in Prussia, there are as many as 19 parties competing.

Havas, Berlin, 23rd – Tomorrow is election day. The atmosphere in the streets of Berlin today is very different than usual. Demonstrations by various parties and deafening music are common. Clashes between the Communist Party and the National Socialist Party are commonplace in the city and cause no surprise. What is more striking is that the windows of the entire city are hung with flags, a dazzling array of colors. The workers' areas of Wedding and Rukin are covered in red flags, with a sickle and hammer representing labor and agriculture painted on them. The Steglitz area, where the National Socialist Party is concentrated, is hung with swastika flags. Other areas have the red flag of the Social Democratic Party, with a red, gold, and black symbol in the upper corner. They are everywhere. There are also many residences where the residents on the upper and lower floors belong to different parties, so the flags hanging on the windows of each floor are different from each other, and arguments often occur because of this. It is said that political parties are buying people to hang flags, with each window with a flag being given one mark per day, which is why there are so many flags.

Reuters, London, 23rd – Both Germany and Austria are currently busy with elections. According to news from Vienna, although the Austrian elections tomorrow are only for the provincial councils, the results are worth noting, as the strength of the various parties after the 1930 parliamentary elections can be determined from this. The Vienna election results are the focus of particular attention. Since the founding of the republic, Vienna has been the base of the Socialist Party. Tomorrow, Germany will hold elections in four states, with the most noteworthy being the state of Prussia. National Socialist Party leader Hitler is doing his best to win a majority of seats in Prussia. According to news from Berlin, Hitler will indeed win more seats this time, but he may not be able to win a majority.

100 US Battleships Prepared to Participate in Spring Maneuvers 66

Shakespeare Theatre Completed 71

British Prince Personally Performs Opening Ceremony

Interior Equipment is the Best in All of England

Reuters, London, 23rd – Stratford-upon-Avon, the birthplace of the great poet Shakespeare, has always had a Shakespearean theatre to commemorate him. It was destroyed by fire several years ago. Later, through public donations, the theatre was rebuilt. The design was publicly competed for, and the design submitted by Ms. Scott was selected. The equipment is extremely complete and is the best of all theatres in England. The opening ceremony was held today. The British Prince flew from London to the theatre. In the afternoon, he opened the doors of the newly built Shakespeare Memorial Theatre with a golden key. At that time, the church bells rang, and flags were hung everywhere to celebrate. Local men and women paraded through the streets wearing costumes from the era of Queen Elizabeth. They danced around the Memorial Theatre, and the City Council also held a tea party to entertain visitors. The famous Shakespearean actor Sir Benson gave a speech at the event. Cabinet member Baldwin and the US Ambassador to the UK also gave speeches. The funds for rebuilding this theatre were donated by lovers of Shakespeare's plays all over the world, especially from the United States. Visitors believe that the new building is flawless in terms of aesthetics and comfort. The theatre has an attached restaurant and a large promenade overlooking the scenery of the River Avon. National News Agency, London, 23rd – Tonight, the first play to be performed will be [Henry IV, Part 1]. The theatre is located in a beautiful forest, surrounded by a small stream, and the scenery is excellent. The new equipment inside the theatre is also comprehensive.

Literary Inquisition of Chinese Students Studying in the US 72

Master's Thesis Written Carelessly

All Students Are Trying to Rescue Him

National News Agency, California, 23rd – All students at the University of California here are now raising money for Chinese student Wei Minghua (transliteration) to send him to Germany or other European countries to save his life. Wei recently submitted a thesis titled [The Communist Party of China] in order to obtain a master's degree from the University of California. He was arrested by the authorities and sentenced to be sent back to his home country. Wei's friends say that Wei's repatriation will likely lead to his death. Later, University of California President Sproul learned of this and did not oppose the students' fundraising for Wei. According to university officials, Wei's thesis only described the historical and theoretical aspects and was not illegal.

Washington's Grandniece Still Alive 74

National News Agency, Munich, Germany, 23rd – After news of the 200th anniversary of the birth of the great American founding father Washington spread to Germany, it was learned that Washington still has a grandniece living in the world, the Countess of Butler-Cloneburg, who currently resides here. She is 88 years old, still healthy and robust. Her grandfather and George Washington were brothers. He returned to Europe 150 years ago and settled in the Netherlands. Her father, Vicomte Washington, was on good terms with Bavarian King Ludwig I, so he moved here, served as Minister of the Court, and was ennobled. The Countess is married to the Count of Butler-Cloneburg.

Important News 75

The Fall of Zhangzhou in Detail 76

Zhang Zhen's Troops Abandon Defense Areas Repeatedly

Bandits Occupy Zhangzhou Without Firing a Single Shot, Xiamen Shocked and on Full Alert

Fuzhou Correspondence: After Zhang Zhen's troops abandoned Longyan and retreated to Shizhong, it has been rumored here that Zhangzhou was occupied by Sun Lianzhong's rebel troops and the Red Army's Lin Biao and other units for two or three days. On the 19th, the provincial government's telegram to Zhangzhou suddenly failed. As of 7 PM on the 20th, military and political authorities had not received confirmation from Zhang Zhen regarding Zhangzhou. However, business circles received a telegram from Xiamen reporting that Zhangzhou had fallen on the afternoon of the 19th, and that Zhang's troops had retreated to Jiangdong Bridge and Songyu, 20 li away from Zhangzhou. It also said that the number of people coming to Xiamen from Zhangzhou had surged to 10,000 in one day. Xiamen Commander Lin Guogeng also telegraphed the provincial government on the evening of the 19th, reporting that Zhang Zhen had sent his adjutant Wu Hanping to Xiamen around 6 PM that evening to discuss military affairs and talk in detail about the military deployment in Zhangzhou. Wu left Zhangzhou in the afternoon, so the claim that Zhangzhou fell on the afternoon of the 19th is difficult to confirm. However, according to the latest report, Sun Lianzhong's rebel troops launched an attack on Zhangzhou around 12 AM on the 19th, and Zhang Zhen immediately ordered a retreat to Jiangdong Bridge. Zhang's troops in the Nanjiang area also concentrated on Zhangpu. The headquarters was moved to Zhao'an. It is said that Zhang's troops retreated step by step, claiming it was for strategic reasons. Among them, Ruan's regiment moved its defense location three times in one day, suffering the greatest losses. Sun Lianzhong's rebel troops number over 10,000, flying the banner of the Founding Revolutionary Army, and are not Red Bandits. The reasons are rumored to be varied. Some say that the Red areas of Jiangxi are thousands of miles of desolate land with a shortage of salt, so Sun's troops wanted to enter Zhangzhou for food, taking advantage of the situation. Others say that the bandits demanded a certain amount of donations from Zhang's troops. The bandits wanted 800,000, but Zhang Zhen only agreed to 200,000, so the bandits attacked out of anger. Still others say that the bandits' purpose was to loot Zhangzhou and Quanzhou and then move towards Shantou. After receiving the report, the provincial government telegraphed the national government and the Military Affairs Commission to report the situation and telegraphed Guangdong, urging it to send a large force to assist in the suppression. At the same time, the Security Office sent Cheng Shichun and Wang Ping and others to Shanghai on the Yongyu Wheel yesterday (20th) to welcome Fang Shengtao back to Fujian to take charge. Starting on the 19th, Xiamen was ordered by Commander Lin to cut off sea traffic and ordered the guard unit and a part of the land force sent from the province to Xiamen to be on full alert. The Chuyu warship stationed in Xiamen was anchored in Songyu to prevent accidents. The Majiang Command also sent Haichou to Xiamen to increase defense. The Navy Department also considered the defense of Xiamen important and decided to send Chen Jiliang to Xiamen to deploy forces. It is also heard that the national government, at the request of overseas compatriots from Fujian, will send Zhu Shaoliang to aid Fujian. At the same time, Chen Jitang will be urged to take up the post of deputy commander of bandit suppression in the border area and lead his troops to Fujian to suppress bandits to secure the region. (20th)

Fuzhou Traitorous Merchant Assassinated 77

Liu Yinghui Passes Off Japanese Cloth as Chinese Cloth

Fuzhou Correspondence: Liu Yinghui, the manager of Datong Foreign Cloth Shop on Shanghang Street, is 36 years old and lives at No. 6 Wu Cuo Alley, Shanghang Street. When anti-Japanese sentiment was tense, he served as a standing committee member of the Fuzhou Merchants Anti-Japanese Association and a design committee member of various Anti-Japanese Associations. Since the Anti-Japanese Association was dissolved, Liu has been privately selling Japanese cloth, falsely selling it as Chinese cloth. For the past month, he has received warning letters, but he has ignored them. At 11 PM on the 17th of this month, Liu had already gone to bed when suddenly four youths in Western attire knocked on the door forcefully. After his family opened the door, they entered the hall and said they were visiting Liu. His wife told them he was asleep. The four men said they had important matters to discuss and barged into the room, dragging Liu from the bed to the hall. Seeing the bad situation, Liu immediately shouted that things could be discussed, why did they have to be like this? Before he finished speaking, one of the men drew a pistol and shot Liu in the back of the head twice. Liu immediately fell to the ground and died. The four men then went out together and fled towards the end of the alley. At that time, Liu's family only consisted of his mother, wife, concubine, and young daughter. Seeing the unexpected, they were at a loss. Around 12 AM, Liu's concubine ran to the Shanghang Street police station to report the incident. The station immediately sent a patrol officer to lead the police to investigate. When they arrived at the entrance of Wu Cuo Alley, they saw a car parked there. They asked the driver, who said it belonged to Tian Tanghua Transport Company and had recently carried four guests here. After the guests got out of the car, they asked him to wait a while and took off a coat, leaving it in the car. Unexpectedly, they never returned. The patrol officer immediately escorted the driver Chen Ce, along with the car and coat, back to the station and then went to Liu's house to investigate, but found no other clues. On the morning of the 18th, a notice from the Youth National Salvation Corps suddenly appeared in the city, saying that the traitorous merchant Liu Yinghui, daring to violate public opinion and privately set up an organization to specialize in trafficking in large quantities of inferior goods during the crisis of a strong enemy's misconduct and the urgency of the national crisis, had repeatedly ignored warnings. The corps believes that it is necessary to impose severe sanctions. Now, in accordance with Article 9 of the Corps Law, he is sentenced to death as a warning to those who do not know how to love the country. Now the military and police detectives are searching for the murderers in all directions, but it is unknown whether they will be able to apprehend them. (April 19)

Hu Hanmin Discusses the Issue of Constitutional Government 78

The Implementation of Constitutional Government Should Emphasize Genuineness Over Speed

Hong Kong Correspondence: Recently, the call for the implementation of constitutional government has been very loud, and various parties have sent letters and telegrams to seek his opinion. Hu Hanmin has issued the following statement: [Recently, in various places such as Beijing, Tianjin, and Shanghai, there is a group of people who advocate ending party rule and implementing constitutional government, believing that the current state of affairs is all the fault of party rule, and that only by implementing constitutional government immediately can the nation's strength be concentrated to cope with this serious national crisis. Whether this argument is logically sound is beside the point. However, in recent days, various parties have sent letters and telegrams to solicit my opinion on this issue, so I cannot remain silent. I believe that, according to the Party's principles, the realization of constitutional government is the sole goal of our Party's revolution for decades. Therefore, the Chinese Nationalist Party does not oppose constitutional government and is the only group that promotes and facilitates constitutional government. I have explained this in detail in the explanatory memorandum of the Outline of Political Tutelage, which I issued when I returned from Europe in 1928, based on Mr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. Although things have not gone as planned in recent years, the Party's will and my personal views have never changed due to various obstacles. Outsiders do not understand and often believe that the Party's use of party rule for political tutelage is the same as party dictatorship, which is baseless. From the perspective of political science, what history has shown us is that the purpose of a national government must involve the people. Therefore, the success of a country and a government is related to the welfare of all the people. That is why we do not tolerate any tyranny and do our best to oppose the monarchical politics of the Qing Dynasty and the dictatorial politics of the warlords. The only reason is that such politics must exclude the majority and take the interests of individuals or a few people as the interests of the country. Since everyone has the same desires, at least the minimum satisfaction must be given to these desires. The right to participate in politics is one of the means of achieving this minimum degree of satisfaction. Mr. Sun Yat-sen advocated the people's rights, the politics of the people, by the people, and for the people. Therefore, I firmly believe that the implementation of constitutional government is not only the inevitable destination of modern politics but also the natural demand of the people. However, what we should pay serious attention to is that in the implementation of constitutional government, we should emphasize its genuineness rather than its speed. People often think that once a country has a constitution written on paper, the great task of constitutional government is accomplished. If this is the case, then all the warlords and bureaucrats of the past and even recently have already done it, so why should we argue about it today? I believe that to implement true constitutional government, we must take the Three Principles of the People, that is, the principles of the people, by the people, and for the people, as the content of the constitution, and we must take local self-government as the foundation of constitutional government. At the same time, we should enrich all single-item laws and regulations to establish the scale of the rule of law. Article 14 of the Outline of National Reconstruction states that after the establishment of a local self-government government in each county, it may elect one national representative to organize a representative assembly to participate in central political affairs. Article 16 states that when all the counties in a province have achieved complete self-government, the constitutional government period begins. Article 22 states that the draft constitution should be based on the achievements of the Outline of National Reconstruction and the periods of political tutelage and constitutional government, and be deliberated by the Legislative Yuan and disseminated to the people at any time for adoption and implementation. All of the above is sufficient to be the basis of my consistent views. In the past three years, I have formulated legislative guidelines and devoted myself to legislative work, and I have always followed this. Some may suspect that I am blinded by party views and cling to what the Outline of National Reconstruction says. In fact, anyone who has not forgotten the history of the Republic of China should know that what Mr. Sun Yat-sen said in the Outline of National Reconstruction is a necessary path to achieving true constitutional government. The declaration of the First National Congress has made a thorough explanation based on past facts, saying, "Since the first year of the Republic of China, there have been constitutions, but the remnants of autocracy, warlords, and bureaucrats have usurped power and committed all kinds of evils. The constitution is no different from waste paper, what can it do to protect the people's rights? Recently, Cao Kun bribed illegally and occupied the position in Beijing, and also used the so-called constitution as a tool for decoration, but what he did was as different from the constitution as a horse's neck is from an ox's. Therefore, we know that the prerequisite for promoting the constitution is whether the people can support the constitution. If the people are not organized, even if there is a constitution, the people themselves cannot use it. Even without the destruction of the warlords, it would still be a formality." Therefore,

Constitutionalists only know how to demand a constitution, without considering how to protect the constitution or how to use the constitution. It can be seen that they have no organization, no system, and no courage to truly implement the constitution. What they said can still be used to evaluate today's facts. As for how we will use the paths mentioned in the Outline of National Reconstruction in the future to move towards true constitutional government, I will discuss it separately. Based on the above, I will repeat: We not only do not oppose constitutional government, but we will do our best to realize constitutional government. However, we do not emphasize the speed of the implementation of constitutional government, but its genuineness. I hope that those who care about the issue of constitutional government will pay attention to this.

Newspaper Reports that Japan is Funding the Construction of the Russian-Indian Railway 79

Exchanging Manchurian Interests with Russia

Kobe Shimbun, according to a trade correspondent from Karachi, reported to the Ministry of Commerce and Industry that representatives from Soviet Russia, Balochistan, Afghanistan, and Japanese capitalists are discussing the construction of a railway from Russia through Afghanistan to the Indian border, and using this railway as a center, extending it northward to connect with the Turkish Siberian Railway, and extending it southward to reach the port of Penderbai in the Gulf of Balochistan. The capital for this railway construction will be provided by Japan in exchange for Russia's transfer of its interests in Manchuria to Japan.

Russia Has No Foreign Policy 80

Statement by People's Commissar Litvinov

600,000 Troops Only Used to Defend Against Aggression

Kobe Shimbun reported that the Russian representative to the Disarmament Conference and People's Commissar for Foreign Affairs Litvinov said to reporters in Geneva a few days ago that Russia had to be on guard on its border because Japan had sent a large army of 70,000 to Manchuria. However, the Moscow government still maintains friendly feelings towards Japan. However, due to the untrustworthiness of its Far Eastern allies, Russia has to be concerned. Russia has no so-called foreign policy. Today, we are not influenced by external emotions in our peaceful relations with the world, but only seek to develop our own destiny. The 600,000 troops that Russia currently has will be used to defend against external invaders. For the sake of self-defense, we believe that 600,000 troops are indispensable. As for economic issues, Russia is self-sufficient and does not need to seek external help. What is most worrying is that Russia will inevitably be drawn into the vortex in the Far East in the future. However, Russia hopes that its allies will maintain peace, and is willing to conclude the non-aggression treaty that was previously proposed.

Jiangsu Provincial Normal School to Become Independent 81

When Jiangsu Provincial Middle School was reorganized in the 16th year [of the Republic, likely 1927], it adopted a combined middle school and normal school system. Most senior high school normal classes were combined with senior high school general classes in one school. Only Huaiyin Rugao Middle School specialized in normal school education. For several years, normal school students and regular middle school students received the same training, and it was deeply felt that efficiency had not increased. Therefore, the independence of normal schools has become an important issue today. The Department of Education previously held a meeting to discuss the independence of normal schools and planned to start implementing it in the 21st year [of the Republic, likely 1932]. A resolution was passed in principle to gradually expand the normal school classes based on the history, geography, and environmental relationships of each school. Subsequently, when formulating the outline of the provincial education budget for the 21st year, a method was also included to designate several middle schools to specialize in normal school education and not accept senior high school general students, in order to gradually achieve the independence of normal schools. This was approved by the provincial government meeting. Now, five detailed measures have been formulated: (1) Starting from the 21st year, the independence of normal middle schools in the province will be completed in three years. (2) Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Taicang, Huaiyin, Donghai, Rugao Middle Schools, and Suzhou Women's and Xuzhou Women's Middle Schools, etc., eight schools, are designated as schools specializing in normal school education. (3) Starting from the 21st year, the aforementioned eight designated schools will no longer enroll new senior high school general students, and other schools will no longer enroll new senior high school normal school students. (4) The original senior high school general students in the designated schools specializing in normal school education and the original senior high school normal school students in other schools will all continue until graduation. (5) The class levels and funding allocation for each school in the 21st year will be separately compiled and ordered to be followed. The notice has been issued to all junior and senior high schools to comply. After three years, the normal schools in the province can be completely independent.

However, the creditor representatives believed that the liquidation should be designated by the court to be legal, so they refused to participate. After the provincial government received the joint report from the Departments of Finance, Education, Industry, and Fourth, it believed that the documents and records of the Songjiang Bank should be transferred to the court. It instructed the county government and approved the case. County Magistrate Shen Jie followed the order. The court has received the Song Bank's documents and records and sealed the bank's premises. Regarding whether the directors engaged in corruption, the provincial order instructed the county to transfer the three directors, Zhang, Ni, and Zhou, to the court with a written statement at 10:00 AM on the 23rd. Regarding public funds, the provincial order designated County Magistrate Shen as the general representative of the public fund creditors, responsible for pursuing legal procedures.

Hong Kang Pawnshop Arson Case: No Evidence Found 88

Insured for 52,000 Taels

Insurance Companies Still Investigating

The Hong Kang Pawnshop on Tokyo Road in Western Shanghai suddenly caught fire at 2:00 AM on February 27 this year. After the fire brigade rushed to the scene and extinguished the fire, most of the buildings and goods had been burned, with losses amounting to more than 50,000 yuan. Subsequently, 160 customers, including Xu Gongxia, accused the pawnshop's manager, Zhang Gengsheng, of arson for fraudulent purposes. They hired lawyer Xi Ya'fu to file a lawsuit with the First Special District Court. After one interrogation, it was ordered to postpone the case because more witnesses needed to be summoned. The matter was recorded in this newspaper. The day before yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Tingqi continued the hearing in the second criminal court. The defendant, Zhang Gengsheng, still appeared in court with his lawyers Yuan Yang'an and Zhang Hengshan. Witness Dai Yuanyuan testified that he was the insurance department director at Ning Shao Insurance Company. Hong Kang Pawnshop held fire insurance with this company for 20,000 taels of silver. After the fire, the next day, he entrusted Yizhong Appraisal Firm to investigate the losses and the cause of the fire. He has not yet received Yizhong's report, so he could not say anything in detail. However, on that day, he went to the Putuo Road Police Station to investigate the cause of the fire and whether there was arson. The police station said that no evidence of arson had been found. Ge Jichen, the manager of Yizhong Appraisal Firm, testified that he was entrusted by Ning Shao and Yong'an Insurance Companies and sent staff to investigate at 10:30 AM on February 27. Sanyi Appraisal Firm had arrived earlier and jointly sorted out the remaining items. They asked the police station about any evidence of arson. The police said that they could not find any evidence and would notify them if any evidence was found in the future. He received a letter from the police station on the 11th of this month after seeing in the newspaper that the Hong Kang Pawnshop had been sued by the customers. He submitted the reply letter and the photos taken at the fire scene at that time. He also stated that Hong Kang Pawnshop held fire insurance for 52,000 taels with various insurance companies. After reviewing the pawnshop's ledger, the value of the pawned silk and leather clothing was more than 50,000 yuan, which, together with the two-point interest, totaled 59,945 yuan, consistent with the insurance amount. E. Arnold, the British manager of the Lao Gongmao Insurance Company, testified that Hong Kang Pawnshop had taken out fire insurance with them for 22,000 taels. After the fire, he went to investigate, but the investigation was still ongoing and had not concluded. The cause of the fire could not be determined, but it did not appear to be arson, and it was likely a careless fire. Watson, the British manager of Sanyi Appraisal Firm, testified that he was entrusted by Lao Gongmao and Sincere Insurance Companies and went to inspect on that day. Because most of the goods had been burned, valuation was extremely difficult and could only be determined based on the ledger. No evidence of arson was found. Liang Guohua and Lu Ruizhi, representatives of Sincere and Yong'an Insurance Companies, submitted a statement that Hong Kang Pawnshop had taken out fire insurance for 50,000 taels with each company. After the fire, they did not go to investigate but entrusted the appraisal firm to handle the matter. They had not yet received a report from the appraisal firm, so they had nothing to say. Judge Wu Tingqi reviewed the statements and ordered that the case be adjourned for further hearing. The defendants were dismissed.

Clever Girl Captures Rickshaw Puller with a Plan 89

Spends Two Hours

Finally Traps the Thief

Shen Xiulan, a girl from Qingjiang, is only thirteen years old, petite and exquisite, and very clever. Her father, Shen Zhengfu, could not farm due to famine and hardship, but possessed martial skills, so he abandoned his sickle and hoe and joined the army. Recently, he had gone to war without regard for his own safety, and his beloved daughter had no one to care for. So, Shen sent Xiulan to be a child bride in the home of a relative in Nanyang Bridge a few days ago. Xiulan had only been in Shanghai for ten days. The day before yesterday, she borrowed two gold coins and a pair of trousers from a relative on Pingji Road and asked Xiulan to retrieve them. She packed them in a small bundle, hired a rickshaw pulled by Wu Xuetai to return home. When the rickshaw arrived at Nanyang Bridge, Xiulan got off to pay the fare. Unexpectedly, Wu took advantage of her youth and snatched the bundle and fled without a trace. Xiulan was very clever. Since her aunt was not as caring as her mother, she was afraid of being beaten, so she did not dare to go home and vowed to find the rickshaw puller. After two hours, she saw the rickshaw puller near the Great World amusement center. Because there were no police officers there, she was afraid of being outnumbered, so she devised a plan. She pretended not to recognize him and hired him to go to the West Gate. Wu had already seen the girl and hesitated, shaking his head to indicate that he would not pull her. The girl said, "Hire your rickshaw, pay you money, why not go?" The rickshaw puller thought that she was not the girl whose belongings had been stolen, so he bargained with her. The girl deliberately lowered the price to 100 cash and took him to the police booth in Nanyang Bridge, where she called the police and had Wu arrested in the second district and sent to the court for investigation.

Last Week Gold Prices Continue to Strengthen 96

Eight Consecutive Weeks of Gains Totaling Eighty-Three Taels

The standard gold price has seen drastic fluctuations over the past four weeks. The surging waves could not be suppressed, with daily rises and falls of over ten taels, a tortuous and confusing situation that left people terrified and without any sense of certainty. This was truly influenced by the divergent trends in overseas silver markets. In England, prices rose, while in America, they remained stable. Starting from the beginning of the week, prices initially rose and then fell, followed by a sudden surge. On Wednesday morning, prices briefly rose to 725.8 taels before a sudden and sharp decline. This was due to frequent news reports about the United States planning to raise exchange rates to the 1926 level or potentially abandoning the gold standard. Prices quickly broke through the 700-tael mark, plunging to a low of 699 taels. Furthermore, the complex international situation led to Shanghai's exchange rates for British pounds remaining stable and American dollars remaining steady, while the exchange rates initially fell and then rose, with minor fluctuations reported. As a result, gold prices entered a state of fluctuation, with speculators and major players pursuing different strategies for buying and selling, engaging in mutual control. However, by the end of the week, a bullish trend reemerged, pushing prices beyond 710 taels. Over the course of the week, there was a total swing of 26.8 taels. Overall, prices rose by 6.9 taels, marking eight consecutive weeks of gains totaling 83.4 taels. Compared to the opening price of 712.5 taels on the first day of the market, there was also an increase of 1.7 taels. The exchange rates for British and American currencies fell by a total of 2.25 and 1.875 points, respectively, leading to a slight increase in the forward premium. The domestic market remained flat, while the American exchange rate tightened. The gold industry experienced various opinions and disputes, but generally, bearish sentiment prevailed. As for the spot standard gold, the Central Bank continued to absorb it, and its price was lower than the June futures. The initial price difference was around 60 taels, later reaching over 80 taels before settling around 70 taels. The exchange rate hedge spread was approximately 40 taels. A Butcher Worthy of Praise 106

— Yi Qiu

During the January 28th Incident, the Japanese invaders used North Sichuan Road as a base. Japanese soldiers coming and going were all high-spirited, as if this road was already their private property, arbitrarily plundering and rampaging wildly. Anyone with a little bit of spirit couldn't help but feel righteous indignation and wish to contribute their lives to repay the country. My friend Qi Jun talked about the story of a butcher on North Sichuan Road. Although it belongs to the past, it is still touching and admirable, and illuminates the nation. I will record it here to enrich this talk.

A certain butcher ran a pork shop at the north end of North Sichuan Road. He was generous by nature, happy to help those in need, and loved to drink. Every evening, he would drink heavily in his shop. After the incident, he sent his wife and son to the countryside. Because business was slow during the war, he told his two apprentices to return home temporarily. Then he stayed to guard the shop. One day, he happened to be very drunk and saw more than ten Japanese soldiers blocking a Chinese woman on the road, making jokes and teasing her. He was greatly angered. He shouted to the Japanese, "Since a man cannot join the army to kill the enemy, he should also sacrifice himself to repay the country, so as not to waste this magnificent seven-foot body!" After shouting, he held the beef-eared knife that he usually used, jumped to the center of the road, and with a wave of his hand, a Japanese soldier died instantly. At first, the Japanese soldiers did not expect this to happen. When they saw that one of their companions had fallen in a pool of blood, they fought him in groups. Before long, the butcher killed six more people in a row. The remaining people, seeing that they could not defeat him, quickly blew their whistles. Japanese police gathered in large numbers, shooting fiercely. The butcher was hit by several bullets and fell with a smile. Alas, how heroic!

World Small Things 107

— Hai Ke

The Fat Queen on a Small Island East of the Fiji Islands in the South Pacific, there is a cluster of small islands called Tonga. Tonga can be considered the smallest kingdom in the world. The queen of the country, called Salote Tupou, can be considered the fattest and biggest queen in the world. She is six feet six inches tall measured barefoot and weighs three hundred pounds. Usually, she wears very little clothing, with more exposed parts. When the country holds some grand ceremony, she must wear a long robe of white rat skin, with a crown on her head, and wear many bejeweled ornaments. She rules three hundred and eighty-five miles of land and twenty-six thousand five hundred and eighty-seven people. Because it belongs to the UK, she was conferred by the British King as a noblewoman of the British Empire.

Shanghai War and Weapons (19) 108

— Yi Zang

Lights Out We want to prevent the enemy planes from ravaging us. During the day, issue air raid alerts to warn all parties. At the same time, send fighter planes to attack enemy planes. At night, use very strict control of lights. What is called lights out? It is to install light control in the vicinity of military ports. Except for the necessary lights, all other lights are completely extinguished. At the same time, use searchlights to detect enemy planes. In the mouths of military ports, set up anti-aircraft guns and machine guns. When enemy planes come, use smoke to cover the military ports. At the same time, fearing that enemy planes will drop poison gas bombs, organize protection groups. Cooperate with the army to share the fire prevention and poison prevention and other evacuation rescue work. To know the whereabouts of enemy planes in advance, set up airplane watchmen in various places. If enemy planes are found, report to all parties by telegram, telephone, whistle, etc. The purpose of very strict light control is to hide the target of enemy planes' attacks. Therefore, never leak light, lest it be detected by the enemy. Then the enemy planes cannot use their means. Now our country has not paid attention to various facilities. Judging from the enemy planes attacking Suzhou on March 20th and the bombing of the Hangzhou Qiaodong Airport on February 4th, if we had made some preparations beforehand, the enemy planes would definitely not have been able to show their brutality.

Tales of Soldiers and Bandits in Twin Towers (34) 109

— Master of the Hall of Seeking Happiness

Chapter Five: Betrayal Leads to Severance of Ties, Misfortune Brings Encounter with a Generous Stranger, Anger Shuts Down Affection, Planning is Most Difficult, Accepting the Grace of a Beauty is Too Much.

If it were just those common, small-time bandit gangs, who truly overestimated themselves and came looking for trouble, they would certainly be slaughtered, leaving a trail of fallen flowers. This would make them understand that An Family Village is extremely formidable and not to be trifled with. However, while military force is indispensable and bandits must be guarded against, one cannot rely solely on bravery and aggression to subdue people with force. To avoid forging deep, irreconcilable hatred with those reckless villains who fear no death, it is necessary to be somewhat flexible and make some effort to turn enemies into friends. It wouldn't hurt to maintain secret communication with them, exchanging information. As long as future peace is maintained, even if a small amount of tribute is given to them annually or seasonally, or if some convenience is provided in concealing their actions from the authorities, there would be nothing unacceptable about it. Fortunately, the strange phenomenon of local gentry harboring bandits, and good citizens colluding with bandits, had been prevalent for a long time. Moreover, the heroes, shouting the slogan "rabbits don't eat grass near their nests," would gladly do this favor, resulting in a fair exchange and peaceful coexistence.

The person who exerted effort in mediating this was An Yu-tian's paternal uncle, An Da-kui. In their family's elder generation, An Da-cheng was the eldest, and An Da-kui was the third. There was also a second uncle, who had passed away early, leaving behind only a young son. Since he had also lost his mother, An Da-cheng and his wife took him in, treating their nephew as their own son. He was An Yu-tian's younger brother, An Yu-yuan. This An Da-kui did not succeed in his studies at home and preferred to associate with hooligans and rascals in the village. Surprisingly, he got to know the famous bandit chief, Niu Hei-feng. This Niu Hei-feng grew up not far from the neighboring county. He had been mixing with bandits since he was a teenager. Later, he surrendered twice and even served as a formal military officer twice, gradually rising in rank. On the third occasion, he rebelled again, becoming a bandit. He seized many guns and coerced many people, and thus rose to become the biggest gang leader. An Da-kui wanted to get a piece of the military pie. Presumably, during the time when Niu Hei-feng surrendered and became a military officer, they established a connection and even kowtowed together, becoming sworn brothers. After Niu Hei-feng resumed his bandit career, An Da-kui, although he did not follow him up the mountain, still maintained contact through messengers, exchanging information. Therefore, Niu Hei-feng, mindful of this friendship, never harassed An Family Village. An Da-cheng, through his brother's introduction, had also met Niu Hei-feng and greatly approved of An Da-kui's actions, willing to maintain a considerable friendship with Niu Hei-feng. In recent years, An Da-kui had found another opportunity to go out and work in a military position. Coincidentally, a military unit belonging to that organization was stationed in a small market town more than thirty li away from An Family Village.

Puppet Marriage 110

— Gou

Yesterday, I saw in the newspaper that "Pu Yi's eldest sister, Second Princess Yun He, and Zheng Xiao-xu's grandson, Yi Kai, were married in Changchun at 1 PM on the 18th, according to the old Qing dynasty system. At 11 AM that day, the groom, wearing Qing dynasty court attire, followed his uncle, Zheng Chui, along with four attendants sent by the Puppet Government, and swore an oath according to the old system. Pu Yi then took a piece of white silk, signed his name and stamped his seal on it. After the ceremony, at 2 PM, the bride and groom returned home," etc.

The marriage of young men and women is not a strange thing, but the marriage of Pu Yi's sister and Zheng Xiao-xu's grandson is somewhat meaningful. Let's talk about it today. Pu Yi and Zheng Xiao-xu were a bunch of foxes and dogs, and everyone knew they were running dogs of the Japanese and traitors to our country. The new organization of Puppet Manchuria was a live drama of puppets taking the stage. The romantic emperor actually looked like a romantic emperor, and the treacherous imperial relative actually looked like a treacherous imperial relative. But if you look at the back, everything is controlled by one person behind the scenes. These wooden figures are still dancing on the stage with self-satisfaction.

Now, in addition to the big show, there's a small show. Pu Yi's eldest sister, Second Princess Yun He, has married Zheng Xiao-xu's grandson, Yi Kai. If we calculate it this way, Zheng Xiao-xu, who was once slapped by the Japanese, is actually the old imperial relative of Puppet Manchuria. Zheng Chui, who once tasted the flavor of Japanese gun butts, is actually the imperial relative of Puppet Manchuria. The incompetent Zheng Yi Kai is actually the imperial horse of Puppet Manchuria. [The whole family is powerful and enjoys the same fate as the country.] Today, Zheng Xiao-xu can be said to be extremely powerful and extremely glorious. Can it be tolerated?

When the live drama of Puppet Manchuria opened the other day, Pu Yi was nominally the Chief Executive, but Zheng Xiao-xu used the imperial system of three kneels and nine kowtows to pay homage to Pu Yi. At that time, I laughed at this old man for violating the world's trends and insisting on following Xuan Tong to advocate for restoration. It was only when the puppets took the stage that I realized that Zheng Xiao-xu had not kowtowed happily for twenty years and was somewhat uncomfortable. Now that there is a place to kowtow, isn't it satisfying? This time, Yi Kai and Yun He are married, and I think another opportunity to kowtow has arrived, because the imperial sister is marrying a slave, and he must kneel three times and kowtow nine times to express his gratitude.

However, there are two points that I would like to ask Mr. Zheng to pay attention to. The puppet organization in the Northeast is not recognized by our country, and it is not recognized by other countries either. This is not so important, and it can be temporarily [closed and changed the year number]. There is also one point that must be guarded against, that is, the palm of the giant spirit and the taste of Japanese-made gun butts.

Robes and hats are reduced to birds and beasts, literature is submerged in wormwood,

Drums and horns rise all over the sky, wind and clouds move the earth,

Holding soldiers fight in vain, leaving thousands of years of sorrow.

Popular Science

War and Airplanes 114

— Nai Zheng

In land warfare, defense can be set up with hundreds of miles of wire mesh, or sandbags can be piled up and deep trenches dug, and landmines buried; charging cavalry and infantry die before they get close. Even tanks rushing in cannot break through. In naval defense, electric nets can also be placed at the mouths of the coast, and submerged mines can be buried to prevent enemy warships and submarines and torpedoes, etc., but in the air, the area is extremely large and the high altitude is incalculable, making it impossible to defend effectively, and difficult to defend at all. Airplanes can take advantage of this, occupying the high ground and dropping bombs to destroy defenses, covering their own cavalry or infantry charges. Therefore, countries have recently been expanding their air forces, and General Zhang Xueliang of our country, on September 18, 1931, uniquely gifted more than two hundred airplanes to Japan. Airplanes have different uses in war, so they can be divided into bomber planes, fighter planes, and reconnaissance planes. I will now describe them separately below:

(1) Bomber planes are the largest of the three types, being able to carry heavy loads and fly in the air for long periods of time. The fuselage can be equipped with light artillery, machine guns, and bombs, etc. The weight of the bombs dropped ranges from half a ton to a ton (one ton equals two thousand pounds), but ordinary bombs, about one hundred and ten to two hundred and twenty pounds, can carry even more bombs. It is not only used for bombing, but also for long-distance reconnaissance. A typical bomber plane is forty-six feet long from head to tail and sixteen feet high. It can fly up to fifteen thousand seven hundred and forty-eight feet, and can reach more than six thousand five hundred and sixty feet in ten minutes. It can continuously fly for ninety hours. Its speed is only thirty miles per hour. Its own weight is five tons, so it flies very slowly, and when carrying heavy bombs, etc., its movements become even more clumsy and slow. We see the Japanese bomber planes slowly circling a few times before dropping bombs, because they are clumsy and difficult to aim at the target. It is easily chased and shot down by fighter planes, so it is also equipped with machine guns to counterattack, but it can never match the nimbleness of fighter planes, so bomber planes must have one or two fighter planes protecting them before they dare to come out and drop bombs. The one shot down at Zhenru this time was a Japanese bomber plane.

(2) Fighter planes are much smaller than bomber planes, and there are several types, including single-seater and double-seater. They are extremely nimble in flight and very convenient for combat. The latest single-seater fighter planes are equipped with a total of six light machine guns, two on the top and two on each side, and the procedure for adding bullets and firing is very convenient. Typically, they are about eighteen feet long and sixteen feet high. They can fly up to more than twenty-five thousand seven hundred feet, but at such a high altitude, the air is thin, and the driver must have an artificial oxygen respirator. It can rise to more than six thousand five hundred feet in five minutes, which is half as fast as a bomber plane. The speed is one hundred and fifty miles per hour, and the weight is only a little over one ton, but it can only fly continuously for two or three hours. Lieutenant Short, the American aviator who died for human justice, reportedly flew a single-seat fighter plane and shot down six Japanese planes in the skies over Suzhou. There is also a type of double-seat fighter plane, where one person drives the plane and the other person carries a light machine gun, which can be fired arbitrarily in all directions, and can also be fired upwards and downwards, with bullets falling like raindrops downwards.

(3) Reconnaissance planes can scout enemy movements and report to their own troops via radio. They also rely on the excellent modern cameras to take extremely clear pictures of the enemy from airplanes thousands of feet high, which can then be enlarged for easier examination and to calculate attack and defense. In the battle on the Longhai Railway between Jiang and Feng, the Central Air Force's reconnaissance planes took photos of the Feng army's defenses. I saw them in a magazine, and although they were reprinted on paper, they were still clear, with the curves of the trenches, the number of people and horses, and the distance of the gun positions all clearly visible. Jiang's army won a great victory because of the reconnaissance planes. As for their size, speed, and altitude, they are not much different from fighter planes. They can also be equipped with machine guns or carry bombs. For every type of offensive weapon, there is a type of defense. After airplanes were used in war, anti-aircraft artillery was invented to defend against them. Anti-aircraft artillery can be arbitrarily rotated in direction and can fire a large number of bullets in one second. It can also be mounted on cars to chase and shoot down airplanes.

With the rapid progress of modern radio technology, airplanes can fly at high altitudes without being piloted by humans, using wireless power to control the airplane, making it move forward, backward, rise, and descend. The intensity of its bombing and the clarity of its reconnaissance are more convenient and powerful than human piloting. There is also a particularly powerful invention of "light." If an airplane in the air is illuminated by a beam of white light, it will immediately burn into charcoal. If it carries gunpowder bombs, it will explode and scatter, disappearing without a trace, which is truly shocking. However, these military inventions are kept secret by all countries and are still under further research. Has our country also made any inventions, keeping them secret and still under research?

Casual Chat

Bloodshed on the Truck 115

— Wu

For several weeks, A Mao had been ordered by Lao Chuang to drive a truck out, so in the darkness of this late night, he had to drive to the dock to transport goods, which was not an exception, nor was it the first time after the war. As usual, the truck driver A Mao did not carry the goods, he just waited quietly for the truck to be fully loaded, and then drove off at full speed. Now he was sitting in his seat without making a sound, because he was constantly attacked by sleepiness, so he couldn't help cursing and saying…

"Damn it! If you want to sell, do it openly. Why be a treacherous merchant doing it so secretly?"

He didn't know how to solve the national crisis, and he wouldn't be able to draft any plan to save the country, but he had personally seen Japanese soldiers kill our people and burn our houses… All the brutal acts were deeply etched in his memory, so as soon as he mentioned the word "Eastern Ocean," it made him very angry.

Suddenly, a coolie got into the car and sat beside him, so he immediately knew that the goods were fully loaded and he was about to start moving forward. Suddenly, the coolie was wrinkling his nose, smelling the air, as if he had discovered a strange smell. Soon, he said to A Mao…

"Hey! Can you smell it? Where does this bloody smell come from?"

"Humph! Really, I smell it too."

As he spoke, he turned on the ignition, and the engine roared.

"Then, where does this bloody smell come from?" the coolie asked…

"Only God knows…"

The truck had begun to move, bumping along the road.

"Ah! I know," A Mao said again…

"This truck transported wounded soldiers on the front lines, and it's stained with a lot of blood!…"

Finally, he muttered to himself…

"Damn it! The blood of the soldiers hasn't dried yet, but Japanese goods are being imported in large quantities!"

door.

not in my eyes, they're only worth three dollars,

Alas! I'm sorry, please…"

The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Police Department vs. Huang Juchu, Theft Case (Main Text): Huang Juchu, a habitual thief and recidivist, is sentenced to two years imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be counted as two days for one day of imprisonment. Private Plaintiff Zhang Yeshi vs. Li Lin, Bigamy Case (Main Text): This case is not accepted.

Criminal Instruction: A petition from Zhou Zhengshi requesting bail for Zhou Fugao. Having reviewed the petition, Zhou Fugao has already been sent to prison by this court for execution of the sentence. The petitioner's claim that there is a sick person at home and requesting bail is not in accordance with the law and cannot be approved. This is hereby instructed.

Instruction: Sun Fuquan requests the filing of a case regarding Li Zhongyun, et al., absconding. Having reviewed the petition, there is no procedure for filing a criminal case. The request to file a case is not in accordance with the law. You are hereby informed of this instruction. Instruction: Jiang Dechen requests the filing of a case regarding Yu Dexi's threats. Having reviewed the petition, there is no procedure for filing a criminal case. The request to file a case is not in accordance with the law. You are hereby informed of this instruction. Instruction (Above are from the 23rd)
